Indic language text (in the 8 languages currently supported) by listening to the speech output. Hear2Read Apps are also useful for people without Visual Impairment (often referred to as sighted users) as described later.\r\n\r\nIndic Text To Speech (TTS) App provides TTS service to Windows 7 or 10 applications that use Speech APIs (SAPI 5.1) to \"Read\" by \"Hearing\" to software generated speech. The TTS engine runs as a background service similar to eSpeak. Some of the commonly used TTS applications that we know of are:\r\n\r\n-\tNVDA (Non Visual Desktop Access)\r\n-\tTextAloud from NextUp.com\r\n-\tBalabolka from Cross+A (cross-plus-a.com)\r\n-\tDspeech from Dimio.Altervista.org\r\n-\tShare to Speech from Labsii \r\n\r\nWe are working on integrating with Windows 10 Narrator. \r\n\r\nThe TTS App converts Unicode Indic text and ASCII English text to speech. This first release supports the following 8 Indic languages:\r\n\r\n1.\tGujarati female and male voices\r\n2.\tHindi male voice (primarily for Windows 7 users)\r\n3.\tKannada female and male voice\r\n4.\tMarathi male voice\r\n5.\tPunjabi female voice\r\n6.\tSanskrit male voice\r\n7.\tTamil male voice\r\n8.\tTelugu female and male voices\r\n\r\nAfter successful installation of Indic Text To Speech (TTS) App, the installer creates a shortcut for the App on the Desktop.\r\n\r\nThe App User Interface lists the Hear2Read voices installed in the PC. The basic App incudes a English voice. There are two buttons at the bottom of the App window:\r\n\r\n-\tClicking the left button (Listen to a Demo Here) opens a browser window with Hear2Read.org demo. The user can select a voice and listen to TTS output for the selected voice.\r\n\r\n-\tClicking the right button (Get More Voices Here) opens the voice download page on Hear2Read web site where the user can download additional voices. \r\n\r\nAfter adding the voice, the Screen Reading App settings need to be changed to use the Voice as described in the User Guide for the Screen Reading App.\r\n\r\nMost of the TTS applications listed above provide the option to save speech output in an audio file.\r\n\r\nThis App can be used by people who cannot read printed text but understand the spoken language well.\r\n\r\nIt can be used to reduce the load of books that children have to carry to school, as a suitably formatted EBook and this App can replace the printed book.\r\n\r\nPlease send questions and comments to Feedback@Hear2Read.org.\r\n\r\nHear2Read Apps use Festvox, Festival and Flite open source software developed by Carnegie Mellon University (CMU) and collaborators including Hear2Read volunteers and University of Edinburgh.\r\n\r\nNote: Hear2Read is a registered trademark","ProductFamilyName":"Apps","Schema":"Card;1"}],"Title":"Trending","HasThirdPartyIAPs":false,"AlgoName":"RECO-Algo-Version","AlgoValue":"Lists;newAndRising;;Apps;00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000003","TotalItems":973,"PageSize":200}}
